# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
A change of sign indicates a root lies in the interval [0.5, 0.6] AND the graph is continuous ^eXOaa2uB

a) Show that xlnx + x - 3 = 0 has a root in the interval 1 to 2
b) Using a suitable iteration formula find the root to 3sf
c) Show that your root is correct to 3sf ^aJ48buQn
